                                    <div data-testid="PropertyDescription" class="Stack__StackContainer-sc-agfvon-0 ifnOCi">
                                        <div class="Stack__StackContainer-sc-agfvon-0 ifnOCi">
                                            <h2 class="Text__Typography-sc-1103tao-0 cmSYNV">SOLD BY THE DOUGLAS MAY TEAM</h2>
                                            <span class="styles__Address-sc-8e6gfp-1 jhxlCk">52 WIGLOW STREET, WACOL</span>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="styles__PropertyDescriptionBody-sc-8e6gfp-0 bMCuZM">
                                            <div>
                                                <div class="styles__TellMeMoreContainer-sc-1uhsiqq-0 kPqtmW">
                                                    <span id=":R94pr3ld:" class="styles__TellMeMoreText-sc-1uhsiqq-1">
                                                        <p class="property-description__content">Tucked away on a quiet, tree-lined cul-de-sac just moments from the golf course and train station, this low-set brick home on 1,127sqm offers a serene sanctuary for families, downsizers, or those seeking a tranquil tree change.

Surrounded by nature and designed for outdoor enjoyment, the home invites a relaxed lifestyle immersed in greenery. Air-conditioning, plantation shutters, and tiled floors enhance the flowing interiors, which offer a selection of versatile living zones. Host movie nights in the cosy media room or unwind with loved ones in the open-plan lounge and dining area, anchored by a stylish kitchen with a stone island bench and stainless steel appliances.

Step outside to the covered patio and embrace sun-soaked days in the sprawling backyard-perfect for setting up a soccer goal, cricket match, or trampoline. Framed by flourishing gardens, this expansive outdoor retreat includes room for pets to roam and a chicken coop at the rear.

Three bedrooms provide peaceful retreats, including a master suite with a walk-in robe and dual vanity ensuite. A second bathroom with a bathtub and separate toilet caters to the rest of the household, alongside an internal laundry. With a double garage and a huge shed with side access with 4 ton two post hoist, toilet, sink and provision for a shower, power points and lights, there is abundant space for cars, tools, and all your weekend toys.

Property highlights:
- Low-set brick home on a quiet, leafy 1,127sqm
- Open kitchen, living and dining area, separate media room
- Stone kitchen benchtops, stainless steel appliances
- Undercover patio, sprawling backyard, chicken coop
- 3 bedrooms with wardrobes, 2 bathrooms, laundry
- Master suite featuring a walk-in robe and ensuite
- Double-car garage, 7.5x9.0m double-door shed
- Split system air-conditioning, ceiling fans
- LED downlights, plantation shutters, security screens.

Hidden amongst the trees in a private cul-de-sac, this property presents a peaceful lifestyle not to be missed. Featuring Gailes Golf Course, McLeod Country Golf Club, sporting fields and boat ramps just a stone's throw away, you can enjoy recreation, boating and games outdoors in the sunshine.

Shopping, supermarkets, cafes and dining are only 10 minutes away at Metro Middle Park and Mt Ommaney Centre. Offering easy access to schools and transport, Wacol train station is 700m away, and you are moments from the Ipswich Motorway, Carole Park State School and Westside Christian College.

Any personal information provided to Cameron Crouch Property T/As Ray White Sherwood, will come under the terms set out in our Privacy Policy, which can be found here for your convenience: https://www.raywhite.com/privacy.</p>
